## <span style="color:#FFC107">◇ ASSISTANT</span>  *[2026-02-16 11:37:45]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Bash -- Commit team governance feature</summary>

**Input:**

*Commit team governance feature*  

```bash
git commit -m "$(cat <<'EOF'
Add team governance: messaging isolation, role-based ACL, closed teams

Introduces a governance layer with two team types (open/closed), two
privileged roles (MANAGER and Chief-of-Staff), messaging isolation for
closed teams, and ACL guards on team resources.

New files:
- types/governance.ts: TeamType, GovernanceConfig types
- lib/governance.ts: Password mgmt, MANAGER/COS role queries (bcryptjs)
- lib/message-filter.ts: checkMessageAllowed() — unified message filter
- lib/team-acl.ts: checkTeamAccess() — team resource ACL
- app/api/governance/route.ts: GET governance status
- app/api/governance/password/route.ts: POST set/change password
- app/api/governance/manager/route.ts: POST assign/remove MANAGER
- app/api/teams/[id]/chief-of-staff/route.ts: POST assign/remove COS

Modified files:
- types/team.ts: Added type? and chiefOfStaffId? to Team interface
- lib/team-registry.ts: Migration (existing teams → open), extended
  createTeam/updateTeam for type and chiefOfStaffId fields
- app/api/v1/route/route.ts: Message filter before local delivery
- lib/message-send.ts: Message filter before Web UI delivery
- app/api/teams/[id]/route.ts: ACL guards + type/COS in PUT
- app/api/teams/[id]/tasks/route.ts: ACL guards on GET/POST
- app/api/teams/[id]/tasks/[taskId]/route.ts: ACL guards on PUT/DELETE
- app/api/teams/route.ts: Accept type and chiefOfStaffId on create
- install-messaging.sh: Add team-governance to skill install list
- package.json/yarn.lock: Added bcryptjs dependency

Key design: Open teams preserve ALL current behavior. Governance only
applies to closed teams. Web UI requests (no X-Agent-Id header) always
pass ACL checks — only agent-to-API requests are filtered.
EOF
)"
```

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

you must also remember to add a UI control to the agent profile panel to make the agent a MANAGER or a CHIEF-OF-STAFF or (default) a normal agent. In the future there could be more titles, so make the selection from a popup list and ensure only one role at time can be assigned to an agent, and that the roles of MANAGER and CHIEF-OF-STAFF are protected by passwords if someone wants to assign them to an agent. If the manager title is already assigned to some agent, the action of selecting the title of MANAGER should open a dialog popup window showing the current manager and a message like : "Warning: The current manager is agent xxxxx.. do you want to change the current manager from xxxx to this agent? (only one manager can exist)". And then asking for the password if the user select yes instead of cancel. And both MANAGER and Chief Of Staff agents can belong to multiple teams, so the UI should be modified to show multiple teams the agent belongs to, and to add/remove the agent from them, being either open teams or closed teams (only the MANAGER and the CHIEF-OF-STAFF can decide their own closed teams, other agents can only choose to move themselves to a single team from open teams, but they cannot add themselves to closed teams.. only MANAGERs and CHIEFs-OF-STAFF can assign/unassign agents to/from closed teams). Make sure to make the UI coherent with these rules.

     2→Generated: 2026-02-16

    26→```

    54→  }

**Input:**

**Agent:** `Plan` | **Description:** Design governance role UI plan  

Design a detailed implementation plan for adding governance role management UI to the AI Maestro agent profile panel and team management.  

## Context  

AI Maestro has a governance system with:  
- **MANAGER**: Global singleton (stored in `~/.aimaestro/governance.json` as `managerId`)  
- **CHIEF-OF-STAFF (COS)**: Per-team role for closed teams (stored as `team.chiefOfStaffId` on Team objects)  
- **Normal agent**: Default, no special role  
- **Governance password**: Required for MANAGER and COS assignment (bcrypt, min 6 chars)  

The governance BACKEND is complete (4 API routes, library functions, message filter, ACL). No UI exists yet.  

## What Needs To Be Built  

### 1. Role Selector in Agent Profile Panel  
- **Location**: `components/AgentProfile.tsx` (1256 lines), in the Identity section between "Owner/Team" grid and the next section  
- The Identity section currently has: Avatar, Agent Name, Display Label, Owner (free text), Team (free text)  
- Add a **Governance Role** field after the Owner/Tea  
... [6114 more chars]  

**Result:**

Now I have a thorough understanding of the codebase. Let me present the detailed implementation plan.  

---  

## Governance Role Management UI -- Implementation Plan  

### Overview of Current State (VERIFIED)  

**Backend (complete):**  
- `lib/governance.ts` -- GovernanceConfig CRUD, password hashing (bcrypt 12 rounds), manager singleton, COS checks  
- `types/governance.ts` -- `GovernanceConfig { version, passwordHash, passwordSetAt, managerId }`, `TeamType`  
- `types/team.ts` -- `Team { ..., type?: TeamType, chiefOfStaffId?: string }`  
- `app/api/governance/route.ts` -- `GET` returns `{ hasPassword, hasManager, managerId, managerName }`  
- `app/api/governance/password/route.ts` -- `POST { password, currentPassword? }`  
- `app/api/governance/manager/route.ts` -- `POST { agentId, password }` (agentId=null to remove)  
- `app/api/teams/[id]/chief-of-staff/route.ts` -- `POST { agentId, password }` (closed teams only, agentId=null to remove)  
- `app/api/teams/route.ts` -- `GET` returns `{ teams }` with all teams including type and chiefOfStaffId  

**Frontend (nothing governance-related exists):**  
- No `useGovernance` hook  
- No governance dialog components  
- No role badges  
- The Identity section in `AgentProfile.tsx` (lines 403-486) has: Avatar, Agent Name, Display Label, Owner (free text), Team (free text) as a simple 2-col grid  
- Same pattern repeated in `zoom/AgentProfileTab.tsx` (lines 302-367)  

---  

### File Plan  

**New files to create (5):**  

| File | Purpose |  
|------|---------|  
| `hooks/useGovernance.ts` | Hook to fetch governance state + all teams; derives agent role |  
| `components/governance/GovernancePasswordDialog.tsx` | Set initial / confirm existing password |  
| `components/governance/RoleAssignmentDialog.tsx` | Radio-card role picker with password confirmation |  
| `components/governance/RoleBadge.tsx` | Small colored chip/badge for MANAGER / CHIEF-OF-STAFF |  
| `components/governance/TeamMembershipSection.tsx` | Replace free-text Team field; shows real team memberships |

  "limit": 10

**Result:**

     1→# Team Governance: Messaging Isolation, Role-Based ACL, and Closed Teams  
     2→  
     3→## Context  
     4→  
     5→AI Maestro currently has **ZERO authentication or access control** across all team, task, document, and messaging routes. Any agent can message any other agent, join any team, and access any team's kanban/tasks/documents. This creates chaos when multiple agent groups work on different projects -- agents receive irrelevant messages, wrong directives, and can accidentally interfere with other teams' workflows.  
     6→  
     7→This plan introduces a governance layer with two team types (open/closed), two privileged roles (MANAGER and CHIEF-OF-STAFF), messaging isolation for closed teams, and ACL guards on team resources (kanban, tasks, documents).  
     8→  
     9→**Key design principle:** Open teams preserve ALL current behavior. Governance only applies to closed teams.  
    10→  

</details>

The "To" field in the compose form uses a **free-text input with autocomplete suggestions**, NOT a dropdown. Agent selection uses filtering by alias/host with keyboard navigation. The AMP skill provides CLI commands (`amp-send.sh`) that agents use from the terminal, while the web UI calls `/api/messages` POST.  
     7→

    22→- **Forward action:** POSTs to `${apiBaseUrl}/api/messages/forward` with body: `{ messageId, fromSession, toSession, forwardNote }`

---

## Messaging UI Governance Enforcement (files 8-9)

### 8. `components/MessageCenter.tsx` — Recipient filtering

The compose form uses a free-text `<input>` with autocomplete suggestions from `allAgents: AgentRecipient[]`. The governance filter needs to be applied at two levels:

**Level 1: Autocomplete filtering (client-side UX guard)**

The component needs a new API endpoint to know which agents the sender can reach. Add a new API endpoint:

**New file: `app/api/governance/reachable/route.ts`**
- `GET /api/governance/reachable?agentId=<senderAgentId>`
- Returns `{ reachableAgentIds: string[] }` — the list of agent IDs this sender can message
- Uses `checkMessageAllowed()` from `lib/message-filter.ts` to check each registered agent against the sender
- If sender is not in any closed team (open world), returns ALL agents
- If sender is in a closed team, returns only: same-team members + COS + MANAGER (if applicable)
- If sender is MANAGER, returns ALL agents
- If sender is COS, returns: MANAGER + other COS + own team members

In `MessageCenter.tsx`, when composing:
1. Fetch `GET /api/governance/reachable?agentId=<currentAgentId>` on mount (or when compose tab is selected)
2. Filter `allAgents` to only show agents whose `id` is in `reachableAgentIds`
3. If user types a name that matches an unreachable agent, show a **warning badge** next to the suggestion: "This agent is in a closed team you cannot reach"
4. If the user somehow sends to an unreachable agent (types the full name bypassing autocomplete), the backend `sendFromUI()` already blocks it via `checkMessageAllowed()` — the message-send.ts filter we added earlier throws an error, which the UI should display as an inline error message

**Level 2: Send error handling (already partially implemented)**

The `sendFromUI()` function in `lib/message-send.ts` already has the `checkMessage

<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `governance.ts`</summary>

  "file_path": "/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/governance.ts",

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * Governance Library - Password management, manager role, and team role checks  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Storage: ~/.aimaestro/governance.json  
     5→ * Follows the same synchronous file I/O pattern as lib/team-registry.ts  
     6→ */  
     7→  
     8→import fs from 'fs'  
     9→import path from 'path'  
    10→import os from 'os'  
    11→import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs'  
    12→import { loadTeams, getTeam } from './team-registry'  
    13→import type { GovernanceConfig } from '@/types/governance'  
    14→import { DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG } from '@/types/governance'  
    15→import type { Team } from '@/types/team'  
    16→  
    17→const AIMAESTRO_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.aimaestro')  
    18→const GOVERNANCE_FILE = path.join(AIMAESTRO_DIR, 'governance.json')  
    19→  
    20→const BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS = 12  
    21→  
    22→/** Ensure ~/.aimaestro directory exists */  
    23→function ensureAimaestroDir() {  
    24→  if (!fs.existsSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR)) {  
    25→    fs.mkdirSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR, { recursive: true })  
    26→  }  
    27→}  
    28→  
    29→/** Load governance config from disk, creating with defaults if missing */  
    30→export function loadGovernance(): GovernanceConfig {  
    31→  try {  
    32→    ensureAimaestroDir()  
    33→    if (!fs.existsSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE)) {  
    34→      // First-time initialization: write defaults and return them  
    35→      saveGovernance(DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG)  
    36→      return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }  
    37→    }  
    38→    const data = fs.readFileSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE, 'utf-8')  
    39→    const parsed: GovernanceConfig = JSON.parse(data)  
    40→    return parsed  
    41→  } catch (error) {  
    42→    console.error('Failed to load governance config:', error)

**Result:**

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { loadGovernance, setPassword, verifyPassword } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→  
     4→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     5→  try {  
     6→    const body = await request.json()  
     7→    const { password, currentPassword } = body  
     8→  
     9→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string' || password.length < 6) {  
    10→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })  
    11→    }  
    12→  
    13→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    14→  
    15→    // If password already set, require current password  
    16→    if (config.passwordHash) {  
    17→      if (!currentPassword || !verifyPassword(currentPassword)) {  
    18→        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })  
    19→      }  
    20→    }  
    21→  
    22→    setPassword(password)  
    23→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })  
    24→  } catch (error) {  
    25→    console.error('Failed to set password:', error)  
    26→    return NextResponse.json(  
    27→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set password' },  
    28→      { status: 500 }  
    29→    )  
    30→  }  
    31→}  
    32→  

</details>

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { verifyPassword, setManager, removeManager, loadGovernance } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→import { getAgent } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     4→  
     5→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     6→  try {  
     7→    const body = await request.json()  
     8→    const { agentId, password } = body  
     9→  
    10→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string') {  
    11→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    12→    }  
    13→  
    14→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    15→    if (!config.passwordHash) {  
    16→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password not set. Set a password first via POST /api/governance/password' }, { status: 400 })  
    17→    }  
    18→  
    19→    if (!verifyPassword(password)) {  
    20→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid governance password' }, { status: 401 })  
    21→    }  
    22→  
    23→    if (agentId === null) {  
    24→      removeManager()  
    25→      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, managerId: null })  
    26→    }  
    27→  
    28→    if (typeof agentId !== 'string' || !agentId.trim()) {  
    29→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId must be a non-empty string or null' }, { status: 400 })  
    30→    }  
    31→  
    32→    // Verify agent exists  
    33→    const agent = getAgent(agentId)  
    34→    if (!agent) {  
    35→      return NextResponse.json({ error: `Agent '${agentId}' not found` }, { status: 404 })  
    36→    }  
    37→  
    38→    setManager(agentId)  
    39→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, managerId: agentId, managerName: agent.name || agent.alias })  
    40→  } catch (error) {  
    41→    console.error('Failed to set manager:', error)  
    42→    return NextResponse.json(  
    43→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set manager' },  
    44→      { status: 500 }  
    45→    )  
    46→  }  
    47→}

    34→      }

    44→      setTeams(prev => prev.filter(t => t.id !== teamId))  
    45→    } catch (error) {  
    46→      console.error('Failed to delete team:', error)  
    47→    }  
    48→  }  
    49→

    33→}  
    34→  
    35→// Generate a consistent unique avatar URL from agent ID using RandomUser.me  
    36→// RandomUser.me has 100 men + 100 women = 200 unique portraits  
    37→function getAvatarUrl(agentId: string): string {  
    38→  // Hash the agent ID to get a consistent number  
    39→  let hash = 0  
    40→  for (let i = 0; i < agentId.length; i++) {  
    41→    const char = agentId.charCodeAt(i)  
    42→    hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + char  
    43→    hash = hash & hash // Convert to 32-bit integer  
    44→  }  
    45→  
    46→  // Use absolute value and mod to get index 0-99  
    47→  const index = Math.abs(hash) % 100  
    48→  
    49→  // Alternate between men and women based on another bit of the hash  
    50→  const gender = (Math.abs(hash >> 8) % 2 === 0) ? 'men' : 'women'  
    51→  
    52→  return `/avatars/${gender}_${index.toString().padStart(2, '0')}.png`  
    53→}  
    54→  
    55→// Generate a consistent color from a string (for avatar ring/fallback)  
    56→function stringToRingColor(str: string): string {  
 

... [735 more chars truncated]

**Result:**

     1→'use client'  
     2→  
     3→import { X } from 'lucide-react'  
     4→import type { TaskWithDeps } from '@/types/task'  
     5→  
     6→interface DependencyPickerProps {  
     7→  tasks: TaskWithDeps[]  
     8→  selectedIds: string[]  
     9→  onChange: (ids: string[]) => void  
    10→  excludeTaskId: string | null  // Task being edited (can't depend on itself)  
    11→}  
    12→  
    13→export default function DependencyPicker({ tasks, selectedIds, onChange, excludeTaskId }: DependencyPickerProps) {  
    14→  // Filter out the task being edited and already-selected tasks from the dropdown  
    15→  const availableTasks = tasks.filter(t =>  
    16→    t.id !== excludeTaskId && !selectedIds.includes(t.id)  
    17→  )  
    18→  
    19→  const selectedTasks = tasks.filter(t => selectedIds.includes(t.id))  
    20→  
    21→  const handleAdd = (taskId: string) => {  
    22→    if (!selectedIds.includes(taskId)) {  
    23→      onChange([...selectedIds, taskId])  
    24→    }  
    25→  }  
    26→  
    27→  const handleRemove = (taskId: string) => {  
    28→    onChange(selectedIds.filter(id => id !== taskId))  
    29→  }  
    30→  
    31→  return (  
    32→    <div className="space-y-1">  
    33→      <label className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Blocked by</label>  
    34→  
    35→      {/* Selected dependencies */}  
    36→      {selectedTasks.length > 0 && (  
    37→        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">  
    38→          {selectedTasks.map(t => (

  "file_path": "/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/governance/password/route.ts"

**Result:**

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { loadGovernance, setPassword, verifyPassword } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→  
     4→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     5→  try {  
     6→    const body = await request.json()  
     7→    const { password, currentPassword } = body  
     8→  
     9→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string' || password.length < 6) {  
    10→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })  
    11→    }  
    12→  
    13→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    14→  
    15→    // If password already set, require current password  
    16→    if (config.passwordHash) {  
    17→      if (!currentPassword || !verifyPassword(currentPassword)) {  
    18→        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })  
    19→      }  
    20→    }  
    21→  
    22→    setPassword(password)  
    23→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })  
    24→  } catch (error) {  
    25→    console.error('Failed to set password:', error)  
    26→    return NextResponse.json(  
    27→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set password' },  
    28→      { status: 500 }  
    29→    )  
    30→  }  
    31→}  
    32→  

</details>

**Result:**

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { verifyPassword, setManager, removeManager, loadGovernance } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→import { getAgent } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     4→  
     5→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     6→  try {  
     7→    const body = await request.json()  
     8→    const { agentId, password } = body  
     9→  
    10→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string') {  
    11→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    12→    }  
    13→  
    14→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    15→    if (!config.passwordHash) {  
    16→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password not set. Set a password first via POST /api/governance/password' }, { status: 400 })  
    17→    }  
    18→  
    19→    if (!verifyPassword(password)) {  
    20→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid governance password' }, { status: 401 })  
    21→    }  
    22→  
    23→    if (agentId === null) {  
    24→      removeManager()  
    25→      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, managerId: null })  
    26→    }  
    27→  
    28→    if (typeof agentId !== 'string' || !agentId.trim()) {  
    29→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId must be a non-empty string or null' }, { status: 400 })  
    30→    }  
    31→  
    32→    // Verify agent exists  
    33→    const agent = getAgent(agentId)  
    34→    if (!agent) {  
    35→      return NextResponse.json({ error: `Agent '${agentId}' not found` }, { status: 404 })  
    36→    }  
    37→  
    38→    setManager(agentId)  
    39→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, managerId: agentId, managerName: agent.name || agent.alias })  
    40→  } catch (error) {  
    41→    console.error('Failed to set manager:', error)  
    42→    return NextResponse.json(  
    43→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set manager' },  
    44→      { status: 500 }  
    45→    )  
    46→  }  
    47→}  
    

... [3 more chars truncated]

/**  
 * Governance Library - Password management, manager role, and team role checks

 * Storage: ~/.aimaestro/governance.json

import fs from 'fs'  
import path from 'path'  
import os from 'os'  
import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs'  
import { loadTeams, getTeam } from './team-registry'  
import type { GovernanceConfig } from '@/types/governance'  
import { DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG } from '@/types/governance'  
import type { Team } from '@/types/team'  

const AIMAESTRO_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.aimaestro')  
const GOVERNANCE_FILE = path.join(AIMAESTRO_DIR, 'governance.json')  

const BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS = 12  

/** Ensure ~/.aimaestro directory exists */  
function ensureAimaestroDir() {  
  if (!fs.existsSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR)) {  
    fs.mkdirSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR, { recursive: true })  
  }  
}  

/** Load governance config from disk, creating with defaults if missing */  
export function loadGovernance(): GovernanceConfig {  
  try {  
    ensureAimaestroDir()  
    if (!fs.existsSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE)) {  
      // First-time initialization: write defaults and return them  
      saveGovernance(DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG)  
      return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }  
    }  
    const data = fs.readFileSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE, 'utf-8')  
    const parsed: GovernanceConfig = JSON.parse(data)  
    return parsed  
  } catch (error) {  
    console.error('Failed to load governance config:', error)  
    return { ...DEFAULT_GOVERNANCE_CONFIG }  
  }  
}  

/** Write governance config to disk */  
export function saveGovernance(config: GovernanceConfig): boolean {  
  try {  
    ensureAimaestroDir()  
    fs.writeFileSync(GOVERNANCE_FILE, JSON.stringify(config, null, 2), 'utf-8')  
    return true  
  } catch (error) {  
    console.error('Failed to save governance config:', error)  
    return false  
  }  
}

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
import { loadTeams, createTeam } from '@/lib/team-registry'  
import type { TeamType } from '@/types/governance'  

// GET /api/teams - List all teams  
export async function GET() {  
  const teams = loadTeams()  
  return NextResponse.json({ teams })  
}  

// POST /api/teams - Create a new team  
export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
  try {  
    const body = await request.json()  
    const { name, description, agentIds, type, chiefOfStaffId } = body  

    if (!name || typeof name !== 'string') {  
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team name is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    }  

    if (agentIds && !Array.isArray(agentIds)) {  
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentIds must be an array' }, { status: 400 })  
    }  

    const team = createTeam({ name, description, agentIds: agentIds || [], type, chiefOfStaffId })  
    return NextResponse.json({ team }, { status: 201 })  
  } catch (error) {  
    console.error('Failed to create team:', error)  
    return NextResponse.json(  
      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to create team' },  
      { status: 500 }  
    )  
  }  
}

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
import { getTeam, updateTeam, deleteTeam } from '@/lib/team-registry'  
import { checkTeamAccess } from '@/lib/team-acl'  

// GET /api/teams/[id] - Get a single team  
export async function GET(  
  request: NextRequest,  
  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }  
) {  
  const { id } = await params  
  const team = getTeam(id)  
  if (!team) {  
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team not found' }, { status: 404 })  
  }  
  const agentId = request.headers.get('X-Agent-Id') || undefined  
  const access = checkTeamAccess({ teamId: id, requestingAgentId: agentId })  
  if (!access.allowed) {  
    return NextResponse.json({ error: access.reason }, { status: 403 })  
  }  
  return NextResponse.json({ team })  
}  

// PUT /api/teams/[id] - Update a team  
export async function PUT(  
  request: NextRequest,  
  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }  
) {  
  try {  
    const { id } = await params  
    const agentId = request.headers.get('X-Agent-Id') || undefined  
    const access = checkTeamAccess({ teamId: id, requestingAgentId: agentId })  
    if (!access.allowed) {  
      return NextResponse.json({ error: access.reason }, { status: 403 })  
    }  
    const body = await request.json()  
    const { name, description, agentIds, lastMeetingAt, instructions, lastActivityAt, type, chiefOfStaffId } = body  

    const team = updateTeam(id, { name, description, agentIds, lastMeetingAt, instructions, lastActivityAt, type, chiefOfStaffId })  
    if (!team) {  
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team not found' }, { status: 404 })  
    }  

    return NextResponse.json({ team })  
  } catch (error) {  
    console.error('Failed to update team:', error)  
    return NextResponse.json(  
      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to update team' },  
      { status: 500 }  
    )  
  }  
}

  request: NextRequest,  
  { params }: { params: Promise<{

/**  
 * Team Registry - File-based CRUD for team persistence  
 *  
 * Storage: ~/.aimaestro/teams/teams.json  
 * Mirrors the pattern from lib/agent-registry.ts  
 */  

import fs from 'fs'  
import path from 'path'  
import os from 'os'  
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid'  
import type { Team, TeamsFile } from '@/types/team'  
import type { TeamType } from '@/types/governance'  

const AIMAESTRO_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.aimaestro')  
const TEAMS_DIR = path.join(AIMAESTRO_DIR, 'teams')  
const TEAMS_FILE = path.join(TEAMS_DIR, 'teams.json')  

function ensureTeamsDir() {  
  if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_DIR)) {  
    fs.mkdirSync(TEAMS_DIR, { recursive: true })  
  }  
}  

export function loadTeams(): Team[] {  
  try {  
    ensureTeamsDir()  
    if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_FILE)) {  
      return []  
    }  
    const data = fs.readFileSync(TEAMS_FILE, 'utf-8')  
    const parsed: TeamsFile = JSON.parse(data)  
    const teams = Array.isArray(parsed.teams) ? parsed.teams : []  

    // Migration: ensure all teams have a type field (default to 'open')  
    let needsSave = false  
    for (const team of teams) {  
      if (!team.type) {  
        team.type = 'open'  
        needsSave = true  
      }  
    }  
    if (needsSave) {  
      saveTeams(teams)  
    }  

    return teams  
  } catch (error) {  
    console.error('Failed to load teams:', error)  
    return []  
  }  
}  

export function saveTeams(teams: Team[]): boolean {  
  try {  
    ensureTeamsDir()  
    const file: TeamsFile = { version: 1, teams }  
    fs.writeFileSync(TEAMS_FILE, JSON.stringify(file, null, 2), 'utf-8')  
    return true  
  } catch (error) {  
    console.error('Failed to save teams:', error)  
    return false  
  }  
}  

export function getTeam(id: string): Team | null {  
  const teams = loadTeams()  
  return teams.find(t => t.id === id) || null  
}  

export function createTeam(data: { name: string; description?: string; agentIds: string[]; type?: TeamType; chiefOfStaffId?: string }): Team {

  const now = new Date().toISOSt

Loading .zprofile at 11:49:46  
/**  
 * Team Resource ACL — checks whether an agent (or web UI request)  
 * is allowed to access a given team's resources.  
 *  
 * Open teams (type undefined or 'open') impose no restrictions.  
 * Closed teams restrict access to the manager, chief-of-staff,  
 * and team members only.  
 */  

import { isManager } from './governance'  
import { getTeam } from './team-registry'  

export interface TeamAccessInput {  
  teamId: string  
  requestingAgentId?: string // undefined = web UI request (always allowed)  
}  

export interface TeamAccessResult {  
  allowed: boolean  
  reason?: string  
}  

/**  
 * Determine whether the requester may access the team's resources.  
 *  
 * Decision order:  
 *  1. Web UI (no agentId)      → allowed  
 *  2. Team not found           → allowed (caller handles 404)  
 *  3. Team is open / untyped   → allowed  
 *  4. Requester is MANAGER     → allowed  
 *  5. Requester is chief-of-staff → allowed  
 *  6. Requester is a member    → allowed  
 *  7. Otherwise                → denied  
 */  
export function checkTeamAccess(input: TeamAccessInput): TeamAccessResult {  
  // 1. Web UI requests (no X-Agent-Id header) always pass  
  if (input.requestingAgentId === undefined) {  
    return { allowed: true }  
  }  

  // 2. Team not found — let the caller deal with 404  
  const team = getTeam(input.teamId)  
  if (!team) {  
    return { allowed: true }  
  }  

  // 3. Open teams (or teams with no explicit type) have no ACL  
  if (team.type !== 'closed') {  
    return { allowed: true }  
  }  

  // 4. MANAGER role always has access  
  if (isManager(input.requestingAgentId)) {  
    return { allowed: true }  
  }  

  // 5. Chief-of-Staff of this team has access  
  if (team.chiefOfStaffId === input.requestingAgentId) {  
    return { allowed: true }  
  }  

  // 6. Team members have access  
  if (team.agentIds.includes(input.requestingAgentId)) {  
    return { allowed: true }  
  }  

  // 7. Everyone else is denied  
  return { allowed: false, reason: 'Access denied: you are not a member of this clo  

... [13 more chars truncated]  

</details>

     4→  
     5→// GET /api/teams - List all teams  
     6→export async function GET() {  
     7→  const teams = loadTeams()  
     8→  return NextResponse.json({ teams })  
     9→}  
    10→  
    11→// POST /api/teams - Create a new team  
    12→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
    13→  try {  
    14→    const body = await request.json()  
    15→    const { name, description, agentIds, type, chiefOfStaffId } = body  
    16→  
    17→    if (!name || typeof name !== 'string') {  
    18→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team name is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    19→    }  
    20→  
    21→    if (agentIds && !Array.isArray(agentIds)) {  
    22→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentIds must be an array' }, { status: 400 })  
    23→    }  
    24→  
    25→    const team = createTeam({ name, description, agentIds: agentIds || [], type, chiefOfStaffId })  
    26→    return NextResponse.json({ team }, { status: 201 })  
    27→  } catch (error) {  
    28→    console.error('Failed to create team:', error)  
    29→    return NextResponse.json(  
    30→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to create team' },  
    31→      { status: 500 }  
    32→    )  
    33→  }  
    34→}

    13→    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team not found' }, { status: 404 })

    15→  const agentId = request.headers.get('X-Agent-Id') || undefined  
    16→  const access = checkTeamAccess({ teamId: id, requestingAgentId: agentId })

   461→export function updateAgent(id: string, updates: UpdateAgentRequest): Agent | null {  
   462→  const agents = loadAgents()  
   463→  const index = agents.findIndex(a => a.id === id)  
   464→  
   465→  if (index === -1) {  
   466→    return null  
   467→  }  
   468→  
   469→  // Support both new 'name' and deprecated 'alias'  
   470→  // Normalize to lowercase for case-insensitive consistency  
   471→  const newName = (updates.name || updates.alias)?.toLowerCase()  
   472→  const currentName = agents[index].name || agents[index].alias  
   473→  const agentHostId = agents[index].hostId || getSelfHostId()  
   474→  
   475→  // Check name uniqueness ON THIS HOST if being updated  
   476→  if (newName && newName.toLowerCase() !== currentName?.toLowerCase()) {  
   477→    const existing = getAgentByName(newName, agentHostId)  
   478→    if (existing && existing.id !== id) {  
   479→      throw new Error(`Agent "${newName}" already exists on host "${agentHostId}"`)  
   480→    }  
   481→  
   482→    // Also rename the tmux session if it exists  
   483→    if (currentName) {  
   484→      try {  
   485→        const { execSync } = require('child_process')  
   486→        // Check if tmux session exists  
   487→        try {  
   488→          execSync(`tmux has-session -t "${currentName}" 2>/dev/null`)  
   489→          // Session exists, rename it  
   490→          execSync(`tmux rename-session -t "${currentName}" "${newName}"`)  
   491→          console.log(`[Agent Registry] Renamed tmux session: ${currentName} -> ${newName}`)  
   492→        } catch {  
   493→          // Session doesn't exist, that's fine  
   494→        }  
   495→      } catch (err) {  
   496→        console.error(`[Agent Registry] Failed to rename tmux session:`, err)  
   497→        // Don't fail the agent update if tmux rename fails  
   498→      }  
   499→    }  
   500→  }  
   501→  
   502→  // Normalize tags if being updated  
   503→  if (updates.tags) {  
   504→    updates.tags = normalizeTags(updates.tags)  
   505→  }  
   506→  
   507  

... [1391 more chars truncated]  

</details>

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-16 11:54:16]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Design a detailed implementation plan for adding governance role management UI to the AI Maestro agent profile panel and team management.  

## Context  

AI Maestro has a governance system with:  
- **MANAGER**: Global singleton (stored in `~/.aimaestro/governance.json` as `managerId`)  
- **CHIEF-OF-STAFF (COS)**: Per-team role for closed teams (stored as `team.chiefOfStaffId` on Team objects)  
- **Normal agent**: Default, no special role  
- **Governance password**: Required for MANAGER and COS assignment (bcrypt, min 6 chars)  

The governance BACKEND is complete (4 API routes, library functions, message filter, ACL). No UI exists yet.  

## What Needs To Be Built  

### 1. Role Selector in Agent Profile Panel  
- **Location**: `components/AgentProfile.tsx` (1256 lines), in the Identity section between "Owner/Team" grid and the next section  
- The Identity section currently has: Avatar, Agent Name, Display Label, Owner (free text), Team (free text)  
- Add a **Governance Role** field after the Owner/Team row  
- Show current role as a badge/chip (Normal, MANAGER, Chief-of-Staff)  
- Clicking it opens a popup selector with available roles  
- **Only one role can be active at a time**  
- Selecting MANAGER or COS requires governance password  
- MANAGER is singleton: if already assigned, show warning dialog before reassignment  

### 2. Role Assignment Dialogs  
- **RoleAssignmentDialog.tsx**: New component, follows existing Pattern B (animated, framer-motion, z-[70])  
  - Shows list of roles: Normal Agent (default), Chief-of-Staff, MANAGER  
  - Use radio-card pattern (like WakeAgentDialog)  
  - When selecting MANAGER:  
    - If another agent is already MANAGER, show warning: "The current manager is agent XXX. Do you want to change the manager from XXX to this agent? Only one manager can exist."  
    - Confirm requires governance password  
  - When selecting COS:  
    - Must select which closed team(s) this COS will lead  
    - Confirm requires governance password  
  - When selecting Normal:  
    - If agent was MANAGER, requires password to remove  
    - If agent was COS, requires password to remove  

### 3. Password Setup Flow  
- If governance password not set yet (`GET /api/governance` returns `hasPassword: false`), prompt user to set one before any protected operation  
- **GovernancePasswordDialog.tsx**: New component for setting or entering password  
  - Mode 1: "Set initial password" (first time)  
  - Mode 2: "Enter password to confirm" (subsequent operations)  

### 4. Team Membership Display (for MANAGER/COS)  
- MANAGER and COS can belong to multiple teams  
- Replace the simple free-text "Team" field in Identity section with a **Team Membership Section**  
- For normal agents: show their single team (or "No team") + list of open teams they can join  
- For MANAGER/COS: show all teams they belong to, allow add/remove from any team  
- Show team type badge: 🔒 closed / 🌐 open  
- Normal agents: can only join open teams, cannot add themselves to closed teams  
- MANAGER/COS: can join/leave any team includi  

... [4114 more chars truncated]  

</div>

     2→import { loadGovernance } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→import { getAgent } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     4→  
     5→export async function GET() {  
     6→  const config = loadGovernance()  
     7→  const managerName = config.managerId ? getAgent(config.managerId)?.name || null : null  
     8→  return NextResponse.json({  
     9→    hasPassword: !!config.passwordHash,

    11→    managerId: config.managerId,

    13→  })

     2→import { loadGovernance, setPassword, verifyPassword } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→  
     4→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     5→  try {  
     6→    const body = await request.json()  
     7→    const { password, currentPassword } = body  
     8→  
     9→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string' || password.length < 6) {  
    10→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })  
    11→    }  
    12→  
    13→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    14→  
    15→    // If password already set, require current password  
    16→    if (config.passwordHash) {  
    17→      if (!currentPassword || !verifyPassword(currentPassword)) {  
    18→        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })  
    19→      }  
    20→    }  
    21→  
    22→    setPassword(password)  
    23→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })  
    24→  } catch (error) {  
    25→    console.error('Failed to set password:', error)  
    26→    return NextResponse.json(  
    27→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set password' },  
    28→      { status: 500 }  
    29→    )  
    30→  }  
    31→}

    80→// ============================================================================  
    81→// Session Name Helpers  
    82→// ============================================================================  
    83→  
    84→/**  
    85→ * Parse tmux session name to extract agent name and session index  
    86→ * Examples:  
    87→ *   "website" → { agentName: "website", index: 0 }  
    88→ *   "website_0" → { agentName: "website", index: 0 }  
    89→ *   "website_1" → { agentName: "website", index: 1 }  
    90→ *   "23blocks-apps-backend" → { agentName: "23blocks-apps-backend", index: 0 }  
    91→ *   "23blocks-apps-backend_2" → { agentName: "23blocks-apps-backend", index: 2 }  
    92→ */  
    93→export function parseSessionName(tmuxName: string): { agentName: string; index: number } {  
    94→  const match = tmuxName.match(/^(.+)_(\d+)$/)  
    95→  if (match) {  
    96→    return { agentName: match[1], index: parseInt(match[2], 10) }  
    97→  }  
    98→  return { agentName: tmuxName, index: 0 }  
    99→}  
   100→  
   101→/**  
   102→ * Compute tmux session name from agent name and session index  
   103→ * Examples:  
   104→ *   ("website", 0) → "website"  
   105→ *   ("website", 1) → "website_1"  
   106→ *   ("23blocks-apps-backend", 0) → "23blocks-apps-backend"  
   107→ *   ("23blocks-apps-backend", 2) → "23blocks-apps-backend_2"  
   108→ */  
   109→export function computeSessionName(agentName: string, index: number): string {  
   110→  return index === 0 ? agentName : `${agentName}_${index}`  
   111→}

   119→ */

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { loadTeams, createTeam } from '@/lib/team-registry'  
     3→import type { TeamType } from '@/types/governance'  
     4→  
     5→// GET /api/teams - List all teams  
     6→export async function GET() {  
     7→  const teams = loadTeams()  
     8→  return NextResponse.json({ teams })  
     9→}  
    10→  
    11→// POST /api/teams - Create a new team  
    12→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
    13→  try {  
    14→    const body = await request.json()  
    15→    const { name, description, agentIds, type, chiefOfStaffId } = body  
    16→  
    17→    if (!name || typeof name !== 'string') {  
    18→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team name is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    19→    }  
    20→  
    21→    if (agentIds && !Array.isArray(agentIds)) {  
    22→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentIds must be an array' }, { status: 400 })  
    23→    }  
    24→  
    25→    const team = createTeam({ name, description, agentIds: agentIds || [], type, chiefOfStaffId })  
    26→    return NextResponse.json({ team }, { status: 201 })  
    27→  } catch (error) {  
    28→    console.error('Failed to create team:', error)  
    29→    return NextResponse.json(  
    30→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to create team' },  
    31→      { status: 500 }  
    32→    )  
    33→  }  
    34→}  
    35→

    13→    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team not found' }, { status: 404 })  
    14→  }  
    15→  const agentId = request.headers.get('X-Agent-Id') || undefined  
    16→  const access = checkTeamAccess({ teamId: id, requestingAgentId: agentId })  
    17→  if (!access.allowed) {  
    18→    return NextResponse.json({ error: access.reason }, { status: 403 })  
    19→  }  
    20→  return NextResponse.json({ team })  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→// PUT /api/teams/[id] - Update a team  
    24→export async function PUT(  
    25→  request: NextRequest,  
    26→  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }  
    27→) {  
    28→  try {  
    29→    const { id } = await params  
    30→    const agentId = request.headers.get('X-Agent-Id') || undefined  
    31→    const access = checkTeamAccess({ teamId: id, requestingAgentId: agentId })  
    32→    if (!access.allowed) {  
    33→      return NextResponse.json({ error: access.reason }, { status: 403 })  
    34→    }  
    35→    const body = await request.json()  
    36→    const { name, description, agentIds, lastMeetingAt, instructions, lastActivityAt, type, chiefOfStaffId } = body  
    37→

    39→    if (!team) {  
    40→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Team not found' }, { status: 404 })  
    41→    }  
    42→  
    43→    return NextResponse.json({ team })  
    44→  } catch (error) {  
    45→    console.error('Failed to update team:',

    91→export function updateTeam(id: string, updates: Partial<Pick<Team, 'name' | 'description' | 'agentIds' | 'lastMeetingAt' | 'instructions' | 'lastActivityAt' | 'type' | 'chiefOfStaffId'>>): Team | null {  
    92→  const teams = loadTeams()  
    93→  const index = teams.findIndex(t => t.id === id)  
    94→  if (index === -1) return null  
    95→  
    96→  teams[index] = {  
    97→    ...teams[index],  
    98→    ...updates,  
    99→    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),  
   100→  }  
   101→  
   102→  saveTeams(teams)  
   103→  return teams[index]  
   104→}  
   105→  
   106→export function deleteTeam(id: string): boolean {  
   107→  const teams = loadTeams()  
   108→  const filtered = teams.filter(t => t.id !== id)  
   109→  if (filtered.length === teams.length) return false  
   110→  saveTeams(filtered)  
   111→  return true  
   112→}

    34→  
    35→// Generate a consistent unique avatar URL from agent ID using RandomUser.me  
    36→// RandomUser.me has 100 men + 100 women = 200 unique portraits  
    37→function getAvatarUrl(agentId: string): string {  
    38→  // Hash the agent ID to get a consistent number  
    39→  let hash = 0  
    40→  for (let i = 0; i < agentId.length; i++) {  
    41→    const char = agentId.charCodeAt(i)  
    42→    hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + char  
    43→    hash = hash & hash // Convert to 32-bit integer  
    44→  }  
    45→  
    46→  // Use absolute value and mod to get index 0-99  
    47→  const index = Math.abs(hash) % 100  
    48→  
    49→  // Alternate between men and women based on another bit of the hash  
    50→  const gender = (Math.abs(hash >> 8) % 2 === 0) ? 'men' : 'women'  
    51→  
    52→  return `/avatars/${gender}_${index.toString().padStart(2, '0')}.png`  
    53→}  
    54→  
    55→// Generate a consistent color from a string (for avatar ring/fallback)  
    56→function stringToRingColor(str: string): string {  
 

... [113 more chars truncated]

     1→'use client'  
     2→  
     3→import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'  
     4→import type { Team } from '@/types/team'  
     5→  
     6→interface UseTeamResult {  
     7→  team: Team | null  
     8→  loading: boolean  
     9→  error: string | null  
    10→  updateTeam: (updates: { name?: string; description?: string; agentIds?: string[]; instructions?: string }) => Promise<void>  
    11→  refreshTeam: () => Promise<void>  
    12→}  
    13→  
    14→export function useTeam(teamId: string | null): UseTeamResult {  
    15→  const [team, setTeam] = useState<Team | null>(null)  
    16→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)  
    17→  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)  
    18→  
    19→  const fetchTeam = useCallback(async () => {  
    20→    if (!teamId) return  
    21→    try {  
    22→      const res = await fetch(`/api/teams/${teamId}`)  
    23→      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch team')  
    24→      const data = await res.json()  
    25→      setTeam(data.team || null)  
    26→      setError(null)

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { forwardFromUI } from '@/lib/message-send'  
     3→  
     4→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     5→  try {  
     6→    const body = await request.json()  
     7→    const { messageId, originalMessage, fromSession, toSession, forwardNote } = body  
     8→  
     9→    // Validate required fields  
    10→    // Either messageId (local forward) or originalMessage (remote forward) must be provided  
    11→    if ((!messageId && !originalMessage) || !fromSession || !toSession) {  
    12→      return NextResponse.json(  
    13→        { error: 'Either messageId or originalMessage, plus fromSession and toSession are required' },  
    14→        { status: 400 }  
    15→      )  
    16→    }  
    17→  
    18→    // Validate that from and to sessions are different  
    19→    if (fromSession === toSession) {  
    20→      return NextResponse.json(  
    21→        { error: 'Cannot forward message to the same session' },  
    22→        { status: 400 }  
    23→      )  
    24→    }  
    25→  
    26→    // Forward the message  
    27→    const result = await forwardFromUI({  
    28→      originalMessageId: messageId,  
    29→      fromAgent: fromSession,  
    30→      toAgent: toSession,  
    31→      forwardNote: forwardNote || undefined,  
    32→      providedOriginalMessage: originalMessage || undefined,  
    33→    })  
    34→  
    35→    return NextResponse.json({  
    36→      success: true,  
    37→      message: 'Message forwarded successfully',  
    38→      forwardedMessage: {  
    39→        id: result.message.id,  
    40→        to: result.message.to,  
    41→        subject: result.message.subject,  
    42→      },  
    43→    })  
    44→  } catch (error) {  
    45→    console.error('Error forwarding message:', error)  
    46→    return NextResponse.json(  
    47→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to forward message' },  
    48→      { status: 500 }  
    49→    )  
    50→  }

    28→export default function MeetingChatPanel({ agents, messages, onSendToAgent, onBroadcastToAll }: MeetingChatPanelProps) {  
    29→  const [recipient, setRecipient] = useState<string>('all')  
    30→  const [inputText, setInputText] = useState('')  
    31→  const [sending, setSending] = useState(false)  
    32→  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)  
    33→

    45→      if (recipient === 'all') {

     1→# Agent Messaging Protocol (AMP)  
     2→  
     3→Send and receive messages with other AI agents using the Agent Messaging Protocol.  
     4→  
     5→---  
     6→  
     7→## ⚠️ IMPORTANT: Identity Check (Run First)  
     8→  
     9→**Before using any messaging commands, ALWAYS verify your identity:**  
    10→  
    11→```bash  
    12→amp-identity  
    13→```  
    14→  
    15→If you see "Not initialized", run:  
    16→```bash  
    17→amp-init --auto  
    18→```  
    19→  
    20→This identity check is essential because:  
    21→- Your AMP identity persists across sessions  
    22→- After context reset, you need to rediscover who you are  
    23→- Each agent has its own isolated AMP directory with identity, keys, and messages  
    24→  
    25→**Your identity file location:** `${AMP_DIR}/IDENTITY.md` (per-agent, auto-resolved)  
    26→  
    27→---  
    28→  
    29→## Overview  
    30→  
    31→AMP is a secure messaging protocol for AI agents. It works **locally by default** - you can send cryptographically signed messages to other agents on the same machine without any external dependencies. Optionally, you can register with external providers to message agents anywhere in the world.  
    32→  
    33→## Quick Start  
    34→  
    35→### 1. Initialize (first time only)  
    36→  
    37→```bash  
    38→amp-init --auto  
    39→```  
    40→  
    41→### 2. Send a message  
    42→  
    43→```bash  
    44→amp-send alice "Hello" "How are you?"  
    45→```  
    46→  
    47→### 3. Check inbox  
    48→  
    49→```bash  
    50→amp-inbox  
    51→```  
    52→  
    53→## Address Formats  
    54→  
    55→**Local addresses** (work within your AI Maestro mesh):  
    56→- `alice` → `alice@<your-org>.aimaestro.local`  
    57→- `bob@acme.aimaestro.local` → Local delivery within acme organization  
    58→  
    59→The organization name is automatically fetched from AI Maestro during initialization.  
    60→  
    61→**External addresses** (require registration):  
    62→- `alice@acme.crabmail.ai` → Via Crabmail provider  
    63→- `backend-api@23block

   452→  // Handle keyboard navigation in autocomplete  
   453→  const handleToKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {  
   454→    if (!showAgentSuggestions || filteredAgents.length === 0) return  
   455→  
   456→    switch (e.key) {  
   457→      case 'ArrowDown':  
   458→        e.preventDefault()  
   459→        setSelectedSuggestionIndex(prev =>  
   460→          prev < filteredAgents.length - 1 ? prev + 1 : prev  
   461→        )  
   462→        break  
   463→      case 'ArrowUp':  
   464→        e.preventDefault()  
   465→        setSelectedSuggestionIndex(prev => (prev > 0 ? prev - 1 : -1))  
   466→        break  
   467→      case 'Enter':  
   468→        e.preventDefault()  
   469→        if (selectedSuggestionIndex >= 0) {  
   470→          selectAgent(filteredAgents[selectedSuggestionIndex])  
   471→        }  
   472→        break  
   473→      case 'Escape':  
   474→        setShowAgentSuggestions(false)  
   475→        break  
   476→    }  
   477→  }  
   478→

    10→  
    11→/**  
    12→ * Fetch with timeout support for mobile messaging  
    13→ */  
    14→async function fetchWithTimeout(  
    15→  url: string,  
    16→  options: RequestInit = {},  
    17→  timeoutMs: number = MESSAGE_API_TIMEOUT  
    18→): Promise<Response> {  
    19→  const controller = new AbortController()  
    20→  const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), timeoutMs)  
    21→  
    22→  try {  
    23→    const response = await fetch(url, {  
    24→      ...options,  
    25→      signal: controller.signal  
    26→    })  
    27→    clearTimeout(timeoutId)  
    28→    return response  
    29→  } catch (error) {  
    30→    clearTimeout(timeoutId)  
    31→    if (error instanceof Error && error.name === 'AbortError') {  
    32→      throw new Error(`Request timed out after ${timeoutMs / 1000}s`)  
    33→    }  
    34→    throw error  
    35→  }  
    36→}
